namespace $ {
  export class $gd_kit_sync_qeue<Item> extends $mol_object {
    protected items = [] as Item[]

    send(item: Item) {}

    flush() {
      let item
      while ( item = this.items.at(0) ) {
        this.send(item)
        this.items.splice(0, 1)
      }
      this.schedule_reset = null
    }

    schedule_reset = null as undefined | null | false

    @ $mol_mem
    protected schedule(next?: null | false): $mol_after_frame | null {
      if (next === false) return null
      return new this.$.$mol_after_frame($mol_wire_async(() => this.flush()))
    }

    add(item: Item) {
      this.items.push(item)
      this.schedule(this.schedule_reset)
      this.schedule_reset = undefined
    }
  }
}

    @ $mol_mem
    current(next?: null) { return this.qeue.at(0) }

    input() {
      const current = this.current()
      current?.audio_data()
      return current ? [ current.audio_node() ] : []
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    playing(next?: boolean) {
      let sample

      this.current()

      while (sample = this.qeue.at(0)) {
        if (next === false) {
          sample.audio_node().active(false)
          this.qeue = []
          return false
        }

        this.output()
        sample.audio_node().wait()
        this.qeue.splice(0, 1)
        this.current(null)
      }

      return true
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    playing(next?: boolean) {
      const sample = this.current()
      if (! sample) return false

      if (next === false) {
        sample.audio_node().active(false)
        this.qeue = []
        return false
      }

      this.output()
      sample.audio_node().wait()

      if (!this.qeue.length) return false

      new this.$.$mol_after_frame(()=> {
        this.qeue.splice(0, 1)
        this.current(null)
      })

      return true
    }

    @$mol_mem
    override Placeholder() {
      const rad_page = super.pages().find(page => page instanceof $gd_kit_frame_page)
      return rad_page ?? super.Placeholder()
    }

    @$mol_mem
    override pages() {
      const pages = super.pages().filter(page => ! (page instanceof $gd_kit_frame_page))

      if (this.rad_card_id()) pages.push( this.Rad_page() )
      if (this.avatar_enabled()) pages.push(this.Avatar())
      if (this.bot_id()) pages.push(this.Chat_page(), ...this.chat_subpages())

      return pages
    }

    protected processing() {
      let blob
      while(blob = this.blobs.at(0)) {
        try {
          this.on_data(blob)
        } catch (e) {
          if ($mol_promise_like(e)) $mol_fail_hidden(e)
          const err = e instanceof Error ? e : new Error(String(e))
          err.cause = blob
          this.processing_error([ err ])
        }
        this.blobs.shift()
      }

      this.schedule_promise = null
    }

    protected schedule_promise = null as Promise<unknown> | null

    protected on_data_event(e: BlobEvent) {
      this.blobs.push(e.data)

      if (this.schedule_promise) return

      this.schedule_promise = $mol_wire_async(() => this.processing())()
    }
